<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окрик.html>о́крик</a> (11681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окрик.html>о́крик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ókrik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окрик.html>о́крика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окрик.html>о́крики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окрик.html>о́криков</a></b>)

***округ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>округ</a> (3543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">округъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okrugŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*okrǫgъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ob-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krǫgъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">circle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>о́круг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ókrug</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>о́круга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>округа́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>округо́в</a></b>), <a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>округа</a> (okrugá) <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>district, okrug</li>
<li>subprefecture <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of Japan</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> circuit</li></ol>

***округлить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a> (17446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krúglyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okruglítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to round <i>(off)</i>, to make round
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кругли́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kruglítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">okrugljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(numbers)</i> to round <i>(off)</i> <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okruglítʹ</b> v bolʹšuju stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньшую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okruglítʹ</b> v ménʹšuju stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>после</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запято́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okruglítʹ</b> do dvux znákov posle zapjatój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round (off) to two decimal places [to the second decimal digit]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(esp. wealth)</i> to increase, to add <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитал.html>капита́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okruglítʹ</b> kapitál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to add to one's capital/wealth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***округлый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:округлый.html>окру́глый</a> (8995)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлый.html>окру́глый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okrúglyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)окру́глее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)окру́глей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rounded</li>
<li>smooth, measured</li>
<li>complete (sentences, etc.)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a> (27071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okruglítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okrugljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округлить.html>округли́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to round <i>(off)</i>, to make round</li>
<li><i>(numbers)</i> to round <i>(off)</i> <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okrugljátʹ</b> v bolʹšuju stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньшую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okrugljátʹ</b> v ménʹšuju stóronu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>зна́ков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>после</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запято́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okrugljátʹ</b> do dvux znákov posle zapjatój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to round (off) to two decimal places [to the second decimal digit]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(esp. wealth)</i> to increase, to add <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:округлять.html>округля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитал.html>капита́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okrugljátʹ</b> kapitál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to add to one's capital/wealth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окружать.html>окружа́ть</a> (3968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружить.html>окружи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okružítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружать.html>окружа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okružátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружить.html>окружи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather round</li>
<li>to encircle, to ring in</li>
<li>to surround, to lavish</li>
<li>to encircle, to round up</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kružítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружить.html>окружи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okružítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружать.html>окружа́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окружной.html>окружной</a> (12492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:округ.html>о́круг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ókrug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружной.html>окружно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okružnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> district</li>
<li>circular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:окружной.html>окружна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okružnája</b> želéznaja doróga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">circular railway; circular railroad; circle line</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окружность.html>окру́жность</a> (15589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружной.html>окружно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okružnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">акру́жнасць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akrúžnascʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружность.html>окру́жность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okrúžnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружность.html>окру́жности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружность.html>окру́жности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окружность.html>окру́жностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>circumference, circle</li></ol>

***октябрь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октя́брь</a> (1728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">октѧбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oktębrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Etymologically, this form is "Octember", and was formed by analogy with the other three month names ending in <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ѧбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ębrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The parallel form <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">октомбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oktombrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">октѫбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oktǫbrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is found in Old Church Slavonic, next to <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">октоврь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oktovrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately borrowed, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ὀκτώβριος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Oktṓbrios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">octōber</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октя́брь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oktjábrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октября́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октябри́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октябре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>October
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:октябрь.html>октябре́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>oktjabré</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in October</span></div></dd>

***окуляр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окуляр.html>окуля́р</a> (8424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Okular</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oculāris</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ocular</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окуляр.html>окуля́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okuljár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окуляр.html>окуля́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окуляр.html>окуля́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окуляр.html>окуля́ров</a></b>)

<ol><li>eyepiece</li>

***окунуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окунуться.html>окуну́ться</a> (12902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окунуть.html>окуну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okunútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окунуться.html>окуну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okunútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окуна́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to plunge <i>(into, in)</i>, to dip <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:окунуться.html>окуну́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja tólʹko <b>okunúsʹ</b> v réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll just dip into the river</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to plunge <i>(into, in)</i>, to become (utterly) absorbed/engrossed <i>(in)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окунуть.html>окуну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okunútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
